pixel haters of today are like brush stroke haters of the beginning of the 20th century it s always difficult to define what new media art is but to me it s not just about being new it s a contemporary way of thinking and responding to the latest tools of creation and changes each generation reveals their own new media art based on current influences and the latest technologies digital is not a term that should be defined as a genre digital is everything in a way new media is more a way of thinking and connecting to the current culture s mode of communicating and i think the phrase digital art is a bad representation with a that is not necessarily of a fine art nature whereas new media has a kind of intellectual definition there s an intellectual connection to the idea of advanced media steven sacks interviewed by andrew m gallery s steven sacks on how to collect new media art in

fitness get reposter scale weight by it goes up and down playing the game of figuring out why may be a temptation sometimes you ll know sometimes you ll guess wrong and sometimes you ll guess right in the end it doesn t really matter sometimes you pee 3 times in a day and don t go number 2 sometimes you go 5 and 2 sometimes you get stressed in all kinds of ways some of which you won t even be aware of like sudden weather changes you re about to get sick or you didn t realize that or on your leg demands more water for normal then healing pickles 0 calories tons of salt water retention eating at different times constipation etc maybe you ate a huge huge meal yesterday for all the right reasons need more this is a complicated but here s the deal if you weigh yourself daily i do this with most clients and you think scale went down 2 pounds today 2 pounds of success scale went up 2 pounds tomorrow 2 pounds of failure scale down 1 pound next day 1 pound of success you re gonna drive yourself insane even if you re truly overweight and the scale going down is truly really important it s still gonna make you think you re failing when your succeeding on many days you don t need that no matter who you are but contrary to what many will say tracking the scale is useful if you want to know if you re in a deficit you wanna know if it s going down if you wanna know if you re losing fat and adding muscle your weight staying the same while waist going down is a good so how do you take your mind on this value sticking to the plan to get the weight off and being the person that will lose the weight and keep it off do that and it will but try not to get caught up with the scale even if you are tracking it daily questions or comments

7 6 early mornings 1 and 2 coconut pancakes woke up early to see the morning alms for the local temples alms take place early in the morning the local monks walk the streets with a basket and offerings normally rice which they will eat as their breakfast for the day alms is a buddhist tradition and in many cases the only way a monk is able to get his meal outside of temple donations we were lucky to find a non tourist street to be able to participate and witness the ceremony in a peaceful manner and saw lines of monks rapidly walking down the street to get from one offering to another since we were up so early we had time to have a tradition big breakfast at the morning market 7am soy and a strong lao style coffee was enough to keep us going for the rest of the day spent the day exploring this town is beautiful and calm and has quickly become one of my top three cities from mount to the river it is set in such a serene environment it s so hard to be stressed here spent the evening watching the sunset over the and enjoying too much food eating a tradition lao meal at pictured one of the smaller monks

day 9 8 a local farmer mentioned to me that i should visit the hut on the property on the valley way an interesting visit as the earth is still so beautifully exposed amazing that this old structure has survived so many generations but there is no information on it i tracked down 90 year old iris morgan pictured with her son owen and had a cup of tea with her in her garden in she lived on the property in the late s for about 7 years with her grandmother mary elizabeth hood at that stage the hut was not functional the children were not allowed near what was called uncle bill s house bill wood had purchased that hut and land when his brother jack moved into iris speaks of the abundant apple and pear trees that grew between the hut and the shed she has no idea of the age of the little hut but her great grandfather william hood purchased that land in the mid 1800 s whether the hut was on the property already or it was built at this stage is unknown one thing for sure is that one little structure has so many stories attached

wat arun ratchawararam ratchawaramahawihan thai or wat arun thai pronunciation w t arun temple of dawn is a buddhist temple wat in bangkok yai district of bangkok thailand on the thonburi west bank of the chao phraya river the temple derives its name from the hindu god aruna often personified as the radiations of the rising sun wat arun is among the best known of thailand 's landmark the first light of the morning reflects off the surface of the temple with pearly iridescence although the temple had existed since at least the seventeenth century its distinctive prang spires were built in the early nineteenth century during the reign of king rama ii cr

coaches tip ever been on a run and it feels more like you 're swimming than running this was most likely caused by a high dew point when considering how fast we should run during the summer we often look at the temperature before we head out the door many of us check the humidity level as well but a major factor when adjusting your pace is dew point the temperature at which water when the dew point is close to the air temp the more the air is this makes it harder for the sweat to off the skin for the desired cooling effect so dew point is a better tool in how your performance is going to be affected check your ego at the door in the summer heat is an intensity just like running a hill if your normal tempo run is on a flat route and you change it one day to an extremely hilly route you probably would end up with a slower overall time for that workout but you 'd say well that was a hilly route that same logic should be applied to a run on a hot humid day on hot humid days pay more attention to effort not pace as long as you feel you put forth the same intensity on a hot humid day as a cooler day do n't worry about what the clock says you 're still getting the same benefit you can use this handy chart to understand when to slow down and what it will feel like outside on your run race every 5 f rise in temperature above 60 f can slow your pace by as much as 10 to 30 seconds per mile and then if you throw in a high dew point forget about running fast just slow down

postcards from somewhere di san ad it was built in 1913 and first used as a rice facility during world war ii occupation forces used the building as a concentration camp for the and killing of political and a transit camp for jews most of whom were then deported to the facilities the only ones built inside a concentration camp in italy were destroyed before the camp was estimate that over 3 000 people were killed in this camp and thousands more imprisoned and transported elsewhere today the former concentration camp operates as a civic museum location via giovanni 5 trieste italy price admission free highly recommended

live in the moment easier said than done how do you live in the now i love to hear how you live in the moment and any tips you have as someone that has lived with depression and anxiety i can say i have lived in the past or the future fare to much here is a couple of things i do to push my self to the now my meditation 1 make my bed the first thing i do when i get up look feel smell and hear this one minute can be so powerful 2 cleaning i found just doing the cleaning is great as i have a task and i m doing it now i also found i stop thinking about other shit 3 sit down in the past i have sat down in a crazy busy part of the city and just people watched listened to the sounds and i try and focus into a sound like someone singing 4 cooking cooking is great as you have to be in the moment to get things done also so you don t over cook the food 5 eat with friends home cook is best for me as your sharing enjoy the taste of the meal talk listen this can be hard as you can easy go back and forward from future and past but that s only a thought you are with your friends now experience a lovely meal together 6 read watch research this can do a few things for me this can make you learn about my past and how to do things in future but the action is in the moment remember that so look it as learning exploring and enjoying the moment thanks for taking the time to read love to hear any kind words

together we are stronger thanks for being part of klassik international the klassik generation klassik international the klassik generation is our generation an artistic movement of xxi century that involves professionals and awesome persons who contribute to life that we are compromised in this life and preserve human values klassik international the klassik generation a movement that brings together artists of different genders at the international level artists painters creative directors art directors video games designers photographers dj s musicians singers designers industrial designers interior designers architects athletes worldwide champions and legends fashion designers haute cuisine s chefs digital artists writers actors film directors executive producers politicians investors property developers etc throughout the centuries there has been a great diversity of artistic movements usually inspired and influenced by the social and economic moment that surrounded them each generation has tried to convey their feelings fears joys or worries in different ways with different styles klassik international the klassik generation is our generation an artistic movement of xxi century that involves professionals and awesome persons who contribute to life who are compromised in this life and preserve human values who dedicate our lives for it who are committed in this life for what we do for what we create for what we dream for what we believe for what we fight for the legacy we leave in this life and that will pass from generation to generation thanks for being part of klassik international the klassik generation laura klassik copyright laura klassik
